When we arrived at the hotel, two or three concierges at the entrance of the hotel were playing with their mobile phones instead of entertaining customers. The importance of concierge is far greater than many people think. The concierge represents the first impression, if the concierge is not good then the guest will not be satisfied with the hotel in the first place.
As our check-in time was around 11:00 noon, the room was not available, told us to call before 3:00 to let us know. These are OK, but the front desk forgot to ask a very important point: whether you want a non-smoking room.
After notifying us that the room was cleaned at 2:30, we took our room card and went to room 6923. We smelled a strong smell of cigarettes, and felt that a guest had smoked at least one pack of cigarettes that morning. We went back to the front desk and asked to change rooms and

It is clear that life requires a non-smoking room, but the front desk actually told 6923 that it is a non-smoking room. A non-smoking room has such a strong smell of smoke, shouldn‚Äôt the room manager ask the reason for the cleaning? And shouldn‚Äôt the air freshener be used to remove the smell of smoke? What‚Äôs even more outrageous is that the second non-smoking room 7313 still smells of smoke. Two consecutive non-smoking rooms smell of smoke. As a person who smells cigarettes and wants to throw up, I can't accept it at all. At this time, the manager said that this hotel does not have any management and punishment measures for smoking in non-smoking rooms, and there is no no-smoking sign in the room. Why didn‚Äôt you remind us not to smoke? The manager explained that Northeast people love to smoke and can‚Äôt control it, but I have never seen Northeast people smoke on the plane or high-speed rail, so I don‚Äôt quite accept this explanation.
While waiting for the new room, I saw that many people who checked in were told that the room was still being cleaned and needed to wait. It was already 3:40 at that time. If you can‚Äôt get the room card when you check in after 3:00, you are not eligible. .
Fortunately, the handling method at the front desk is recognized after all: upgrade the room type + free double breakfast. It can show that the hotel still has a sense of service and has a positive attitude in dealing with problems, which is worthy of praise. So actually, I didn't want to write a bad review until I saw this suite room.
I have never seen a five-star hotel with such poor sanitation, which is worse than ordinary express hotels and homestays. There were dirty marks and hairs on the quilt cover, so I asked the cleaning depar**ent to come over and change it. As a result, the cleaning aunt didn't ring the door bell.

I came in by myself, and after changing a set, there were still holes. Crazy chipped walls, dirty tabletops, dusty floors, scratched hair dryers, dirty showers. If you tell me that this room has not been lived in or cleaned for a month, I will believe it. I just want to say that in terms of hygiene, one point is the lower limit of Ctrip, not your lower limit of Shenyang Conrad. If possible, I would like to give 0 points or even negative points.
Some aspects of the room facilities are also very bad. For example, the night lights on both sides must be turned on and off at the same time, the curtains on both sides must be turned on and off at the same time, and the doors on both sides must also be turned on and off at the same time. Does the person who designed the hotel learn geometry or have obsessive-compulsive disorder? Why do they like symmetry so much? There are also table sockets The computer plug cannot be plugged in, the hair dryer has a low wind speed and high temperature, which is not as good as Atour‚Äôs hair dryer, and the sofa collapses when you sit on it, etc.
The breakfast is not bad, but it is far from the level of Conrad, not even the Hilton in the south, nor the newly opened Marriott in North Station. And some waiters in the restaurant are also very unprofessional. After guiding the customers to sit for breakfast for two days, they didn't ask if they want coffee or tea. This is also very unprofessional.
When I write a bad review for a hotel, I don't want everyone to go to a certain hotel to avoid lightning, but I hope that this hotel can properly solve its own problems. As the most luxurious hotel in Shenyang and even in Northeast China, your hotel has attracted many foreign guests. Your hotel is now the business card of the city of Shenyang, and you should use your own actions to make a good impression on this city for tourists from other provinces and foreign countries. Therefore, I propose the following suggestions to the hotel:

1. Strengthen the training of the professional ability of employees in various depar**ents. It is obvious that the business capabilities of a certain depar**ent are flawed.
2. Reorganize the cleaning depar**ent. This level of hygiene is already very explosive in any Hampton and garden, let alone Conrad. And at 3:40pm there are many rooms that have not been cleaned, neither efficient nor quality. 3. Change those weird designs in the facility.
4. Set up clear and strict penalties for smoking in non-smoking rooms, place them in conspicuous places in each non-smoking room, and install smoke alarms.
